# TarotNow Antigravity Audit Errors
Scan time: 2026-04-07 (Asia/Ho_Chi_Minh)

## Rule 2 - Domain Layer

## Rule 18 - Tailwind Best Practices (Anti-Duplication)

### 18.1 `className` không đi qua `cn()`
